Evaluate¶

, (Evaluation Metric) . Bike Sharing Demand Root Mean Squared Logarithmic Error (RMSLE) .

$$ \sqrt{\frac{1}{n} \sum_{i=1}^n (\log(p_i + 1) - \log(a_i+1))^2 } $$

($a_i$, actual) ($p_i$, predict) . (log(count + 1) )

log transformation count(log_count) , log(count + 1) . , log(count + 1) .

$$ \sqrt{\frac{1}{n} \sum_{i=1}^n (p_i - a_i)^2 } $$

Root Mean Squared Error (RMSE) . numpy, scikit-learn RMSE .

In [23]:
# numpy  .
#   (linear algebra)  ,
#   '    '  .
import numpy as np

# scikit-learn  metrics  make_scorer   .
#       scikit-learn     .
from sklearn.metrics import make_scorer

# RMSE    .
#   (predict) (actual)  .
def rmse(predict, actual):
    # predict actual numpy array .
    #        .
    predict = np.array(predict)
    actual = np.array(actual)

    #   predict actual   .
    #   distance    .
    distance = predict - actual
    
    #   distance .
    #   square_distance    .
    square_distance = distance ** 2
    
    #   square_distance  .
    #   mean_square_distance    .
    mean_square_distance = square_distance.mean()
    
    #   mean_square_distance (sqrt) .
    #   score    .
    score = np.sqrt(mean_square_distance)
    
    # score  .
    return score

# scikit-learn make_scorer 
# rmse  scikit-learn      .
#   rmse_score    .
rmse_score = make_scorer(rmse)
rmse_score
Out[23]:
make_scorer(rmse)

Case 1 - Grid Search¶

Grid Search . Cross Validation . ( )

scikit-learn GridSearchCV , Grid Search .

In [25]:
# Gradient Boosting Machine  XGBoost .
#  xgb  .
import xgboost as xgb

# scikit-learn  model_selection   cross_val_score   .
#   Cross Validation .
from sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score

# n_estimators  .
#     ,    (Overfitting)  .
#      .
n_estimators_list = [100, 300, 1000]

# max_depth  . 10 ~ 90  10  .
max_depth_list = [50, 75, 100]

# learning_rate  .   .
#  10 -n  .
learning_rate_list = [1.0, 0.1, 0.01, 0.001, 0.0001]

# subsample  .    ,    .
# 0.5, 0.75, 1.0 . ( 50%, 75%, 100%  .)
subsample_list = [0.5, 0.75, 1.0]

# colsample_bytree  .    ,    .
# 0.5, 0.75, 1.0 . ( 50%, 75%, 100%  .)
colsample_bytree_list = [0.4, 0.7, 1.0]

# colsample_bylevel  .      ,    .
# 0.5, 0.75, 1.0 . ( 50%, 75%, 100%  .)
colsample_bylevel_list = [0.4, 0.7, 1.0]

# hyperparameter    .
hyperparameters_list = []

#   hyperparameter  .
for n_estimators in n_estimators_list:
    for max_depth in max_depth_list:
        for learning_rate in learning_rate_list:
            for subsample in subsample_list:
                for colsample_bylevel in colsample_bylevel_list:
                    for colsample_bytree in colsample_bytree_list:
                        # XGBRegressor .    .
                        # 1) n_estimators.  .    .
                        # 2) max_depth.  .      .
                        # 3) learning_rate.    .   (overfitting)  ,   (underfitting)  .
                        # 4) subsample.        . 0.0 ~ 1.0        .
                        # 5) colsample_bytree.      feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0          feature .
                        # 6) colsample_bylevel.        feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0           feature .
                        #  XGBRegressor model   .
                        model = xgb.XGBRegressor(n_estimators=n_estimators,
                                                 max_depth=max_depth,
                                                 learning_rate=learning_rate,
                                                 subsample=subsample,
                                                 colsample_bytree=colsample_bytree,
                                                 colsample_bylevel=colsample_bylevel,
                                                 seed=37)

                        # cross_val_score .     .
                        # 1) model.     .
                        # 2) X_train. train  feature .
                        # 3) y_train. train  label .
                        # 4) cv. Cross Validation  (split) .  20   20 .
                        # 5) scoring.   .   RMSE .
                        # ,     (mean)   score    .
                        score = cross_val_score(model, X_train, y_train, cv=20, scoring=rmse_score).mean()

                        # hyperparameter    .
                        hyperparameters = {
                            'score': score,
                            'n_estimators': n_estimators,
                            'max_depth': max_depth,
                            'learning_rate': learning_rate,
                            'subsample': subsample,
                            'colsample_bylevel': colsample_bylevel,
                            'colsample_bytree': colsample_bytree,
                        }

                        # hyperparameter    .
                        hyperparameters_list.append(hyperparameters)

                        # hyperparameter   .
                        print(f"n_estimators = {n_estimators}, max_depth = {max_depth:2}, learning_rate = {learning_rate:.6f}, subsample = {subsample:.6f}, colsample_bylevel = {colsample_bylevel:.6f}, colsample_bytree = {colsample_bytree:.6f}, Score = {score:.5f}")


# hyperparameters_list Pandas DataFrame .
hyperparameters_list = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(hyperparameters_list)

#  hyperparameters_list score   .
# (RMSE score      )
hyperparameters_list = hyperparameters_list.sort_values(by="score")

# hyperparameters_list      .
#  (row, column)  .
print(hyperparameters_list.shape)

# hyperparameters_list  5 .
hyperparameters_list.head()

# Gradient Boosting Machine  XGBoost .
#  xgb  .
import xgboost as xgb

# scikit-learn  model_selection   cross_val_score   .
from sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score

#    .
#  100 .
num_epoch = 100

# hyperparameter    .
coarse_hyperparameters_list = []

# num_epoch    .
for epoch in range(num_epoch):
    # 10 100  (int)    n_estimators  .
    n_estimators = np.random.randint(low=100, high=1000)

    # 2 100  (int)    max_depth  .
    max_depth = np.random.randint(low=2, high=100)

    # 1.0 1-e10(10 -10) (float)     learning_rate  .
    learning_rate = 10 ** -np.random.uniform(low=0, high=10)

    # 0.1 1.0 (float)    subsample  .
    subsample = np.random.uniform(low=0.1, high=1.0)

    # 0.4 1.0 (float)    colsample_bytree  .
    colsample_bytree = np.random.uniform(low=0.4, high=1.0)

    # 0.4 1.0 (float)    colsample_bylevel  .
    colsample_bylevel = np.random.uniform(low=0.4, high=1.0)

    # XGBRegressor .    .
    # 1) n_estimators.  .    .
    # 2) max_depth.  .      .
    # 3) learning_rate.    .   (overfitting)  ,   (underfitting)  .
    # 4) subsample.        . 0.0 ~ 1.0        .
    # 5) colsample_bytree.      feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0          feature .
    # 6) colsample_bylevel.        feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0           feature .
    #  XGBRegressor model   .
    model = xgb.XGBRegressor(n_estimators=n_estimators,
                             max_depth=max_depth,
                             learning_rate=learning_rate,
                             subsample=subsample,
                             colsample_bylevel=colsample_bylevel,
                             colsample_bytree=colsample_bytree,
                             seed=37)

    # cross_val_score .     .
    # 1) model.     .
    # 2) X_train. train  feature .
    # 3) y_train. train  label .
    # 4) cv. Cross Validation  (split) .  20   20 .
    # 5) scoring.   .   RMSE .
    # ,     (mean)   score    .
    score = cross_val_score(model, X_train, y_train, cv=20, scoring=rmse_score).mean()
    
    # hyperparameter    .
    hyperparameters = {
        'epoch': epoch,
        'score': score,
        'n_estimators': n_estimators,
        'max_depth': max_depth,
        'learning_rate': learning_rate,
        'subsample': subsample,
        'colsample_bylevel': colsample_bylevel,
        'colsample_bytree': colsample_bytree,
    }

    # hyperparameter    .
    coarse_hyperparameters_list.append(hyperparameters)

    # hyperparameter   .
    print(f"{epoch:2} n_estimators = {n_estimators}, max_depth = {max_depth:2}, learning_rate = {learning_rate:.10f}, subsample = {subsample:.6f}, colsample_bylevel = {colsample_bylevel:.6f}, colsample_bytree = {colsample_bytree:.6f}, Score = {score:.5f}")


# coarse_hyperparameters_list Pandas DataFrame .
coarse_hyperparameters_list = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(coarse_hyperparameters_list)

#  coarse_hyperparameters_list score   .
# (RMSE score      )
coarse_hyperparameters_list = coarse_hyperparameters_list.sort_values(by="score")

# coarse_hyperparameters_list      .
#  (row, column)  .
print(coarse_hyperparameters_list.shape)

# coarse_hyperparameters_list  10 .
coarse_hyperparameters_list.head(10)

Coarse Search , 5 ~ 10 Random Search . Finer Search .

Coarse Search , 5 ~ 10 .

  • n_estimators = 300 ~ 1,000
  • max_depth = 2 ~ 60
  • learning_rate = 1.0 ~ 0.01
  • subsample = 0.2 ~ 0.7
  • colsample_bytree = 0.7 ~ 1.0
  • colsample_bylevel = 0.4 ~ 1.0

, Random Search .

# 300 1000  (int)    n_estimators  .
n_estimators = np.random.randint(low=300, high=1000)

# 2 60  (int)    max_depth  .
max_depth = np.random.randint(low=2, high=60)

# 1.0 1-e2(10 -2) (float)     learning_rate  .
learning_rate = 10 ** -np.random.uniform(low=0, high=2)

# 0.2 0.7 (float)    subsample  .
subsample = np.random.uniform(low=0.2, high=0.7)

# 0.7 1.0 (float)    colsample_bytree  .
colsample_bytree = np.random.uniform(low=0.7, high=1.0)

# 0.4 1.0 (float)    colsample_bylevel  .
colsample_bylevel = np.random.uniform(low=0.4, high=1.0)

Finer Search

In [38]:
# Gradient Boosting Machine  XGBoost .
#  xgb  .
import xgboost as xgb

# scikit-learn  model_selection   cross_val_score   .
from sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score

#    .
#  100 .
num_epoch = 100

# hyperparameter    .
finer_hyperparameters_list = []

# num_epoch    .
for epoch in range(num_epoch):
    # 300 1000  (int)    n_estimators  .
    n_estimators = np.random.randint(low=300, high=1000)

    # 2 60  (int)    max_depth  .
    max_depth = np.random.randint(low=2, high=60)

    # 1.0 1-e2(10 -2) (float)     learning_rate  .
    learning_rate = 10 ** -np.random.uniform(low=0, high=2)

    # 0.2 0.7 (float)    subsample  .
    subsample = np.random.uniform(low=0.2, high=0.7)

    # 0.7 1.0 (float)    colsample_bytree  .
    colsample_bytree = np.random.uniform(low=0.7, high=1.0)

    # 0.4 1.0 (float)    colsample_bylevel  .
    colsample_bylevel = np.random.uniform(low=0.4, high=1.0)

    # XGBRegressor .    .
    # 1) n_estimators.  .    .
    # 2) max_depth.  .      .
    # 3) learning_rate.    .   (overfitting)  ,   (underfitting)  .
    # 4) subsample.        . 0.0 ~ 1.0        .
    # 5) colsample_bytree.      feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0          feature .
    # 6) colsample_bylevel.        feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0           feature .
    #  XGBRegressor model   .
    model = xgb.XGBRegressor(n_estimators=n_estimators,
                             max_depth=max_depth,
                             learning_rate=learning_rate,
                             subsample=subsample,
                             colsample_bylevel=colsample_bylevel,
                             colsample_bytree=colsample_bytree,
                             seed=37)

    # cross_val_score .     .
    # 1) model.     .
    # 2) X_train. train  feature .
    # 3) y_train. train  label .
    # 4) cv. Cross Validation  (split) .  20   20 .
    # 5) scoring.   .   RMSE .
    # ,     (mean)   score    .
    score = cross_val_score(model, X_train, y_train, cv=20, scoring=rmse_score).mean()

    # hyperparameter    .
    hyperparameters = {
        'epoch': epoch,
        'score': score,
        'n_estimators': n_estimators,
        'max_depth': max_depth,
        'learning_rate': learning_rate,
        'subsample': subsample,
        'colsample_bylevel': colsample_bylevel,
        'colsample_bytree': colsample_bytree,
    }

    # hyperparameter    .
    finer_hyperparameters_list.append(hyperparameters)

    # hyperparameter   .
    print(f"{epoch:2} n_estimators = {n_estimators}, max_depth = {max_depth:2}, learning_rate = {learning_rate:.10f}, subsample = {subsample:.6f}, colsample_bylevel = {colsample_bylevel:.6f}, colsample_bytree = {colsample_bytree:.6f}, Score = {score:.5f}")

# finer_hyperparameters_list Pandas DataFrame .
finer_hyperparameters_list = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(finer_hyperparameters_list)

#  finer_hyperparameters_list score   .
# (RMSE score      )
finer_hyperparameters_list = finer_hyperparameters_list.sort_values(by="score")

# finer_hyperparameters_list      .
#  (row, column)  .
print(finer_hyperparameters_list.shape)

# finer_hyperparameters_list  10 .
finer_hyperparameters_list.head(10)

# Gradient Boosting Machine  XGBoost .
#  xgb  .
import xgboost as xgb

# :        ,
#     . (    )
# best_n_estimators = 859
# best_max_depth = 10
# best_learning_rate = 0.011105
# best_subsample = 0.362207
# best_colsample_bytree = 0.980396
# best_colsample_bylevel = 0.870122

# XGBRegressor .    .
# 1) n_estimators.  .    .
# 2) max_depth.  .      .
# 3) learning_rate.    .   (overfitting)  ,   (underfitting)  .
# 4) subsample.        . 0.0 ~ 1.0        .
# 5) colsample_bytree.      feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0          feature .
# 6) colsample_bylevel.        feature  . 0.0 ~ 1.0           feature .
#  XGBRegressor model   .
model = xgb.XGBRegressor(n_estimators=best_n_estimators,
                         max_depth=best_max_depth,
                         learning_rate=best_learning_rate,
                         subsample=best_subsample,
                         colsample_bytree=best_colsample_bytree,
                         colsample_bylevel=best_colsample_bylevel,
                         seed=37)
